    (function (window, document) {
      var regexApp = function () {
        return /MobApp_Android|MobApp_iOS|MobApp_WP/;
      };

      var getUserAgent = function () {
        if (window.getUserAgent) {
          return window.getUserAgent();
        }
        return window.navigator.userAgent;
      };

      var extractAppFromUserAgent = function () {
        var appUserAgent, appVars, index, ua, userAgentParts;
        ua = getUserAgent();
        userAgentParts = ua.split(' ');
        for (index in userAgentParts) {
          appUserAgent = userAgentParts[index];
          if (regexApp().test(appUserAgent)) {
            appVars = appUserAgent.split('/');
            return {
              name: appVars[0].replace('_', ' '),
              version: appVars[1],
              frameworkVersion: appVars[2]
            };
          }
        }
        return null;
      };

      var addGlbOnAppClass = function () {
        var frameworkVersion, nativeAppInfo;
        nativeAppInfo = extractAppFromUserAgent();
        if (nativeAppInfo !== null) {
          if (nativeAppInfo.frameworkVersion) {
            frameworkVersion = parseInt(nativeAppInfo.frameworkVersion, 10);
            if (frameworkVersion >= 1) {
              document.documentElement.className += ' glb-on-app';
            }
          }
        }
      };

      addGlbOnAppClass(); // Garante que o header irá sumir rápido
    })(window, document);

(function ($, window, undefined){
    "use strict";

    $(function () {
        var popinElement = $('[data-gui-popin=".mais-esportes-popin"]');

        var menuDestaque = $(".widget-menu-destaques");
        var widget = new WidgetMenuDestaques(menuDestaque, {
            quantidade: "16"
        });
        popinElement.on('appended.gui.gui-popin', function () {
            widget.bindSubitemClick();
        });
        widget.init();

        // Dropdown options
        // event trigger changes if we have touch support or not
        var activateEvent = 'click',
            enableOverlay = true;

        // for desktop
        if ($('html').hasClass('no-touch')) {
            activateEvent = 'hover';
            enableOverlay = false;
        }

        new GUI.Tab($('.gui-tab', menuDestaque));
        new GUI.Dropdown(popinElement, {
            activateEvent: activateEvent,
            enableOverlay: enableOverlay,
            mouseoverDelay: 400,
            boundToElement: '.widget-menu-destaques .gui-tab',
            position: "right" // no desktop. no mobile, center
        });
    });

}(jQuery, window));

$(document).ready(function() {
    "use strict";

    if($('.glb-grid-24')){

        var cardId = '#ge-card-classificacao-c68192c5-b9a3-483b-a6cf-e163d3c2e9dc',
                classificacaoFeedReady = false,
                classificacaoCardReady = false;

            $(document).on('bastian-feed-card_rendered', cardId, function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Feed Ready');
                classificacaoFeedReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

            $(document).on('card-classificacao-ready', function() {
                console.debug('Classificacao: Card Ready');
                classificacaoCardReady = true;
                initCardClassificacao();
            });

        var initCardClassificacao = function(){
            if(classificacaoCardReady && classificacaoFeedReady){
                $('#ge-card-classificacao-c68192c5-b9a3-483b-a6cf-e163d3c2e9dc').show();
            }
        }
    }

    try {

      var classificacao = new CardClassificacao({
        context: '#ge-card-classificacao-c68192c5-b9a3-483b-a6cf-e163d3c2e9dc'
      });

      var classificacaoTracking = new CardClassificacaoTracking("c68192c5-b9a3-483b-a6cf-e163d3c2e9dc");

    } catch (err) {}

});
